< review>
Did not have an appt. today.
Yesterday was a congenial experience, although my 11:30AM appointment was delayed, possibly by overbooking by a full hour. The employees Janet. Mary, Veronica and Sandra were very attentive and Dr.Kaur explained my Dental plan very clearly
so I would be able to make an empowered decision on my Dental History.

Regarding my January 29th appointment, It was extremely well handled. Two extractions and installation of an upper plate went very well and I was given instructions for maintenance, e.g. no weight lifting for a week, no straw usage, and only water or juice no carbonation.. I do, however, have some discomfort due to no IB Profen as directed since I have never used medication in my 75 Years on Earth.
I will refer friends and Clients to Dr. Kaur.< /review>

I had a great 1st visit at Suave. All the staff were very pleasant. Dr. Kaur was understanding and very easy to talk with about my fear of pain due to a previous experience at another dentist.  She was very gentle and explained in detail the dental work I would need to have done. She was able to calm my fears about coming back to get the work done at Suave.

Update: I've had several visits now to Suave Dental in Riverbank. I'm excited to share.. Strong free WiFi throughout the camp. We had spot 21 which is all grass (like most of the sites) and large enough for a big tent and 2 cars. There's also very hot showers behind a code locked door and a laundry room. The camp host is very nice and also runs the camp gas station/grocery store. Not a place to let kids just run around, as its clearly stated that all animals and children must be closely watched and handled. There is a camp cat though that wanders through.<//text>

< Text>
I called in last night with some questions about a particular new Mitsubishi Outlander that I was interested in purchasing. I'm not from California, and rather than purchasing locally I heard that The Sourth Coast dealership had some great prices and incentives. The rep that I spoke with was awesome! Very helpful and answered all my questions (other than pricing, which he was going to get back to me on). On the website, many of the vehicles don't have a price, but state 'Please Call'.

I hadn't heard from the rep today, so I call to follow up. The rep that answers the phone was extremely rude, and never gave me a chance to speak. He insisted that I look online for pricing, and after explaining that their website directs guests to call, he just throws out a price that was far higher than expected and says they only sell the sticker price.

I call back later to speak with a different rep (Vincent), and had a very similar experience. I was told that as I wasn't coming in immediately I was wasting his time, and the rep would not give me an idea of the price of the vehicle. Again, he directed me to look online, and after getting a little irritated I explained that their website doesn't offer pricing for the models I was looking for. He resisted completely in giving me any idea of where their prices range. I asked to speak with the employee I first spoke to, and was rudely told that he doesn't work there.

I felt really excited to work with this company in the beginning, but I wouldn't make a purchase from them now - awful customer service.</Text>
